| 依赖 | 版本 | 用途 | 语言 |
|------|------|------|------|
| Arrow | 50+ | 列式内存格式 | Rust |
| Tokio | 1.x | 异步运行时 | Rust |
| Tonic | 0.10+ | gRPC 框架 | Rust |
| Raft | 0.7+ | 一致性协议 | Rust |
| DataFusion | 35+ | SQL 解析/优化参考 | Rust |
| RocksDB | 0.21+ | 嵌入式 KV 存储 | Rust (bindgen) |
| Serde | 1.x | 序列化框架 | Rust |
| Tracing | 0.1+ | 结构化日志 | Rust |
| Prometheus | 0.13+ | 指标导出 | Rust |
| Parquet | 50+ | Parquet 读写 | Rust |

### 1.16.18 本章小结

本章从项目愿景与定位出发，全面阐述了 AE 的核心使命、战略定位、设计哲学、目标用户、竞争格局、价值主张、技术选型、团队构成和开源策略。AE 以"运行时自适应优化"为核心差异化竞争力，通过 Rust+Java 双语言架构实现性能与生态的平衡，以 Pipeline 执行模型取代传统 Volcano 模型，以 PID 反馈控制器实现真正的自适应调度。项目采用 Apache 2.0 开源协议，以社区驱动的方式推动生态建设，同时通过企业版和云托管版实现商业可持续性。

---

# 第2章：整体技术架构

---

## 2.1 架构总览与设计理念

### 2.1.1 架构设计理念

AE 的架构设计遵循以下核心理念：

**理念一：分层解耦**

每一层只依赖其下层提供的抽象接口，不跨层依赖。层间通过定义良好的接口通信，使得每一层可以独立演进和替换。

**理念二：自适应闭环**

架构中嵌入反馈闭环，使得运行时数据能够驱动系统行为的动态调整。

```
自适应闭环架构：

┌──────────┐     ┌──────────┐     ┌──────────┐
│  执行    │────>│  监控    │────>│  分析    │
│  Execute │     │  Monitor │     │  Analyze │
└──────────┘     └──────────┘     └──────────┘
                                       │
┌──────────┐     ┌──────────┐     ┌────┘
│  执行    │<────│  决策    │<────┘
│  Execute │     │  Decide  │
└──────────┘     └──────────┘
```

**理念三：弹性边界**

系统中的每个组件都应具备弹性能力——能够根据负载自动伸缩，根据故障自动恢复，根据资源自动调整。

**理念四：最小特权**

每个组件只拥有完成其职责所需的最小权限和最小知识。这减少了组件间的耦合，提高了安全性和可维护性。

### 2.1.2 架构总览图

```
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│                          AE 整体架构                                     │
│                                                                           │
│  ┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐    │

│  │  ┌──────┐  ┌──────┐  ┌──────┐  ┌──────┐  ┌──────┐            │    │
│  │  │ JDBC │  │ODBC  │  │REST  │  │ CLI  │  │SDK   │             │    │
│  │  └──────┘  └──────┘  └──────┘  └──────┘  └──────┘            │    │

│  └─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘    │
└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
```

### 2.1.3 架构风格

AE 采用以下架构风格的组合：

| 架构风格 | 应用位置 | 理由 |
|----------|----------|------|
| 分层架构 | 整体架构 | 关注点分离、独立演进 |
| 微内核架构 | 执行引擎 | 可扩展、可插拔 |
| 事件驱动架构 | 监控与反馈 | 松耦合、实时响应 |
| CQRS | 元数据管理 | 读写分离、性能优化 |
| Actor 模型 | 调度器 | 并发安全、消息驱动 |

---

## 2.2 五层架构深度解析

### 2.2.1 接入层（Access Layer）

#### 概述

接入层是用户与 AE 系统交互的入口，负责协议适配、认证授权、连接管理和查询路由。

#### 组件架构

#### JDBC 适配器实现

```java
public class AEJDBCDriver implements Driver {
    
    static {
        try {
            DriverManager.registerDriver(new AEJDBCDriver());
        } catch (SQLException e) {
            throw new RuntimeException("Failed to register AE JDBC driver", e);
        }
    }
    
    private static final String JDBC_PREFIX = "jdbc:ae:";
    
    @Override
    public Connection connect(String url, Properties info) throws SQLException {
        if (!acceptsURL(url)) {
            throw new SQLException("Invalid URL: " + url);
        }
        
        AEConnectionConfig config = AEConnectionConfig.parse(url, info);
        
        return AEConnectionBuilder.newBuilder()
            .withCoordinator(config.getHosts())
            .withPort(config.getPort())
            .withDatabase(config.getDatabase())
            .withAuth(config.getAuthType(), config.getUser(), config.getPassword())
            .withTLS(config.isTlsEnabled())
            .withConnectionPool(config.getPoolSize())
            .withQueryTimeout(config.getQueryTimeout())
            .build();
    }
    
    @Override
    public boolean acceptsURL(String url) throws SQLException {
        return url != null && url.startsWith(JDBC_PREFIX);
    }
    
    @Override
    public DriverPropertyInfo[] getPropertyInfo(String url, Properties info) {
        return new DriverPropertyInfo[] {
            new DriverPropertyInfo("user", "Username for authentication"),
            new DriverPropertyInfo("password", "Password for authentication"),
            new DriverPropertyInfo("database", "Default database"),
            new DriverPropertyInfo("queryTimeout", "Query timeout in seconds"),
            new DriverPropertyInfo("poolSize", "Connection pool size"),
        };
    }
}
```

#### 认证授权架构

```
认证流程：

┌────────┐     ┌──────────┐     ┌──────────┐     ┌──────────┐
│ Client │────>│ AuthN    │────>│ AuthZ    │────>│ Query    │
│        │     │ Provider │     │ Engine   │     │ Router   │
└────────┘     └──────────┘     └──────────┘     └──────────┘

AuthN Providers:
┌──────────────────────────────────────────┐
│ ┌──────────┐  ┌──────────┐  ┌──────────┐│
│ │ LDAP     │  │ Kerberos │  │ OAuth2   ││
│ │ Provider │  │ Provider │  │ Provider ││
│ └──────────┘  └──────────┘  └──────────┘│
│ ┌──────────┐  ┌──────────┐              │
│ │ JWT      │  │ Basic    │              │
│ │ Provider │  │ Provider │              │
│ └──────────┘  └──────────┘              │
└──────────────────────────────────────────┘

AuthZ Model (RBAC + ABAC):
┌──────────────────────────────────────────┐
│                                           │
│  Role-Based:                              │
│  ├── admin: 全部权限                      │
│  ├── developer: 查询 + 创建表             │
│  ├── analyst: 只读查询                    │
│  └── operator: 运维操作                   │
│                                           │
│  Attribute-Based:                         │
│  ├── 时间限制: 工作时间可查询              │
│  ├── 数据范围: 只能访问本部门数据          │
│  ├── IP限制: 只能从内网访问               │
│  └── 查询限制: 限制并发查询数             │
│                                           │
│  Fine-Grained:                            │
│  ├── 行级权限: WHERE 条件自动注入         │
│  ├── 列级权限: 敏感列自动脱敏             │
│  └── 数据脱敏: 动态脱敏策略               │
│                                           │
└──────────────────────────────────────────┘
```

#### 连接管理

```java
public class ConnectionManager {
    
    private final ConcurrentMap<String, AEConnection> connections;
    private final ScheduledExecutorService cleanupExecutor;
    private final ConnectionPoolConfig poolConfig;
    
    public ConnectionManager(ConnectionPoolConfig config) {
        this.connections = new ConcurrentHashMap<>();
        this.poolConfig = config;
        this.cleanupExecutor = Executors.newSingleThreadScheduledExecutor(
            new ThreadFactoryBuilder()
                .setNameFormat("connection-cleanup-%d")
                .setDaemon(true)
                .build()
        );
        this.cleanupExecutor.scheduleAtFixedRate(
            this::cleanupIdleConnections,
            config.getIdleCheckInterval().toMillis(),
            config.getIdleCheckInterval().toMillis(),
            TimeUnit.MILLISECONDS
        );
    }
    
    public AEConnection createConnection(ConnectionParams params) {
        String connectionId = generateConnectionId();
        AEConnection connection = new AEConnection(connectionId, params);
        connections.put(connectionId, connection);
        return connection;
    }
    
    public void closeConnection(String connectionId) {
        AEConnection connection = connections.remove(connectionId);
        if (connection != null) {
            connection.close();
        }
    }
    
    private void cleanupIdleConnections() {
        Duration maxIdleTime = poolConfig.getMaxIdleTime();
        connections.entrySet().removeIf(entry -> {
            if (entry.getValue().isIdleFor(maxIdleTime)) {
                entry.getValue().close();
                return true;
            }
            return false;
        });
    }
}
```

#### 查询路由器

```
查询路由策略：

┌──────────┐
│ 查询请求  │
└────┬─────┘
     │
     v
┌──────────┐
│ 查询分类  │
│          │
│ ├── 交互式 (Interactive)
│ │   特征: 简单查询、期望秒级响应
│ │   路由: 低延迟队列 + 优先调度
│ │
│ ├── 批处理 (Batch)
│ │   特征: 大规模数据处理、分钟级
│ │   路由: 高吞吐队列 + 大资源分配
│ │
│ ├── 流处理 (Stream)
│ │   特征: 持续运行、低延迟
│ │   路由: 专用流式队列 + 长期资源
│ │
│ └── 混合 (Mixed)
│     特征: 不确定类型
│     路由: 自适应分类 → 动态路由
└──────────┘
```

#### 错误处理

| 错误类型 | 错误码 | 处理策略 | 重试 |
|----------|--------|----------|------|
| 认证失败 | AUTH-001 | 返回 401 | 否 |
| 权限不足 | AUTH-002 | 返回 403 | 否 |
| 查询语法错误 | SQL-001 | 返回详细错误信息 | 否 |
| 查询超时 | EXEC-001 | 取消查询，返回部分结果 | 可配置 |
| 集群不可用 | CLUSTER-001 | 返回 503，建议重试 | 是 |
| 连接数超限 | CONN-001 | 返回 429，排队等待 | 是 |
| 内存不足 | MEM-001 | 自动 Spill 或降低并行度 | 自动 |

### 2.2.2 协调层（Coordination Layer）

#### 概述

协调层是 AE 的大脑，负责查询编译、计划优化、任务调度、资源管理和元数据管理。协调层采用主从高可用架构，支持多活协调器。

#### 组件架构

```
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│                   协调层架构                           │
│                                                       │
│  ┌──────────────────────────────────────────┐        │
│  │           SQL Engine                      │        │
│  │  ┌────────┐ ┌────────┐ ┌────────┐       │        │
│  │  │Parser  │ │Analyzer│ │Optimizer│       │        │
│  │  └────────┘ └────────┘ └────────┘       │        │
│  └──────────────────┬───────────────────────┘        │
│                     │                                 │
│  ┌──────────────────┴───────────────────────┐        │
│  │           Query Planner                   │        │
│  │  ┌────────┐ ┌────────┐ ┌────────┐       │        │
│  │  │Logical │ │Physical│ │Fragment│       │        │
│  │  │Planner │ │Planner │ │Planner │       │        │
│  │  └────────┘ └────────┘ └────────┘       │        │
│  └──────────────────┬───────────────────────┘        │
│                     │                                 │
│  ┌──────────────────┴───────────────────────┐        │
│  │           Adaptive Scheduler              │        │

│  │  │Queue   │ │Selector│ │Binder  │       │        │
│  │  │Manager │ │        │ │        │       │        │
│  │  └────────┘ └────────┘ └────────┘       │        │
│  │  ┌────────┐                               │        │
│  │  │Feedback│                               │        │
│  │  │Controller│                             │        │
│  │  └────────┘                               │        │
│  └──────────────────┬───────────────────────┘        │
│                     │                                 │
│  ┌──────────────────┴───────────────────────┐        │
│  │           Metadata Manager                │        │
│  │  ┌────────┐ ┌────────┐ ┌────────┐       │        │
│  │  │Catalog │ │Schema  │ │Statistics│      │        │
│  │  │Manager │ │Manager │ │Manager  │      │        │
│  │  └────────┘ └────────┘ └────────┘       │        │
│  └──────────────────────────────────────────┘        │
└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
```

#### SQL 引擎组件

**Parser**

```rust
pub struct SqlParser {
    options: ParserOptions,
}

impl SqlParser {
    pub fn parse_sql(&self, sql: &str) -> Result<Statement, ParseError> {
        let tokens = Tokenizer::new(sql).tokenize()?;
        let mut parser = ParserContext::new(tokens, self.options.clone());
        parser.parse_statement()
    }
    
    pub fn parse_statements(&self, sql: &str) -> Result<Vec<Statement>, ParseError> {
        let tokens = Tokenizer::new(sql).tokenize()?;
        let mut parser = ParserContext::new(tokens, self.options.clone());
        let mut statements = Vec::new();
        while parser.has_more() {
            statements.push(parser.parse_statement()?);
        }
        Ok(statements)
    }
}

pub struct ParserOptions {
    pub dialect: SqlDialect,
    pub enable_unicode_identifiers: bool,
    pub max_identifier_length: usize,
    pub enable_quoted_identifiers: bool,
}

pub enum SqlDialect {
    Ansi,
    Postgres,
    Mysql,
    Hive,
}
```

**Analyzer**

```rust
pub struct Analyzer {
    rules: Vec<Box<dyn AnalysisRule>>,
    metadata: Arc<MetadataManager>,
}

impl Analyzer {
    pub fn analyze(&self, statement: Statement) -> Result<AnalyzedStatement, AnalysisError> {
        let mut context = AnalysisContext::new(statement, self.metadata.clone());
        
        for rule in &self.rules {
            context = rule.apply(context)?;
        }
        
        Ok(context.into_analyzed_statement())
    }
}

pub trait AnalysisRule: Send + Sync {
    fn name(&self) -> &str;
    fn apply(&self, context: AnalysisContext) -> Result<AnalysisContext, AnalysisError>;
}

pub struct TypeCheckRule;
impl AnalysisRule for TypeCheckRule {
    fn name(&self) -> &str { "type_check" }
    fn apply(&self, context: AnalysisContext) -> Result<AnalysisContext, AnalysisError> {
        // Type checking logic
        todo!()
    }
}

pub struct ResolveReferencesRule;
impl AnalysisRule for ResolveReferencesRule {
    fn name(&self) -> &str { "resolve_references" }
    fn apply(&self, context: AnalysisContext) -> Result<AnalysisContext, AnalysisError> {
        // Reference resolution logic
        todo!()
    }
}

pub struct ResolveFunctionsRule;
impl AnalysisRule for ResolveFunctionsRule {
    fn name(&self) -> &str { "resolve_functions" }
    fn apply(&self, context: AnalysisContext) -> Result<AnalysisContext, AnalysisError> {
        // Function resolution logic
        todo!()
    }
}
```

**Optimizer**

```rust
pub struct Optimizer {
    logical_rules: Vec<Box<dyn OptimizerRule<LogicalPlan>>>,
    physical_rules: Vec<Box<dyn OptimizerRule<PhysicalPlan>>>,
    cost_model: Arc<dyn CostModel>,
    config: OptimizerConfig,
}

impl Optimizer {
    pub fn optimize(&self, plan: LogicalPlan) -> Result<PhysicalPlan, OptimizeError> {
        let mut current = plan;
        
        for rule in &self.logical_rules {
            let optimized = rule.apply(current.clone())?;
            if self.is_better(&optimized, &current) {
                current = optimized;
            }
        }
        
        let physical = self.generate_physical_plan(current)?;
        
        let mut physical_current = physical;
        for rule in &self.physical_rules {
            let optimized = rule.apply(physical_current.clone())?;
            if self.is_better(&optimized, &physical_current) {
                physical_current = optimized;
            }
        }
        
        Ok(physical_current)
    }
    
    fn is_better<P: Plan>(&self, new: &P, old: &P) -> bool {
        let new_cost = self.cost_model.estimate(new);
        let old_cost = self.cost_model.estimate(old);
        new_cost < old_cost
    }
}
```

#### 自适应调度器

```rust
pub struct AdaptiveScheduler {
    queue_manager: Arc<QueueManager>,
    selector: Arc<QuerySelector>,
    binder: Arc<TaskBinder>,
    feedback_controller: Arc<FeedbackController>,
}

impl AdaptiveScheduler {
    pub async fn submit_query(&self, query: QuerySubmission) -> Result<QueryId, ScheduleError> {
        let query_id = QueryId::new();
        
        let queue = self.classify_query(&query);
        self.queue_manager.enqueue(queue, query_id.clone(), query).await?;
        
        self.schedule_next().await?;
        
        Ok(query_id)
    }
    
    async fn schedule_next(&self) -> Result<(), ScheduleError> {
        let selected = self.selector.select(self.queue_manager.as_ref()).await?;
        
        if let Some((query_id, query, queue)) = selected {
            let bindings = self.binder.bind(&query).await?;
            self.dispatch_tasks(query_id, bindings).await?;
        }
        
        Ok(())
    }
    
    fn classify_query(&self, query: &QuerySubmission) -> QueueType {
        match query.query_type {
            QueryType::Interactive => QueueType::Interactive,
            QueryType::Batch => QueueType::Batch,
            QueryType::Stream => QueueType::Stream,
            QueryType::Auto => {
                if query.estimated_data_size < DataSize::gb(1) {
                    QueueType::Interactive
                } else {
                    QueueType::Batch
                }
            }
        }
    }
}
```

#### 元数据管理器

```rust
pub struct MetadataManager {
    catalogs: RwLock<HashMap<String, Arc<dyn Catalog>>>,
    schema_cache: Arc<SchemaCache>,
    statistics_manager: Arc<StatisticsManager>,
    version_manager: Arc<VersionManager>,
}

impl MetadataManager {
    pub fn register_catalog(
        &self,
        name: &str,
        catalog: Arc<dyn Catalog>,
    ) -> Result<(), MetadataError> {
        let mut catalogs = self.catalogs.write();
        if catalogs.contains_key(name) {
            return Err(MetadataError::CatalogAlreadyExists(name.to_string()));
        }
        catalogs.insert(name.to_string(), catalog);
        Ok(())
    }
    
    pub fn get_table(&self, table_id: &TableId) -> Result<TableMetadata, MetadataError> {
        if let Some(cached) = self.schema_cache.get(table_id) {
            return Ok(cached);
        }
        
        let catalog = self.get_catalog(&table_id.catalog)?;
        let table = catalog.get_table(table_id)?;
        
        self.schema_cache.put(table_id.clone(), table.clone());
        
        Ok(table)
    }
    
    pub fn get_statistics(&self, table_id: &TableId) -> Result<TableStatistics, MetadataError> {
        self.statistics_manager.get_statistics(table_id)
    }
}
```

### 2.2.3 执行层（Execution Layer）

#### 概述

执行层负责查询的实际执行，包括 Pipeline 构建、算子执行、内存管理、Shuffle 数据交换和状态管理。

#### 组件架构

```
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│                   执行层架构                           │
│                                                       │
│  ┌──────────────────────────────────────────┐        │
│  │         Pipeline Executor                 │        │
│  │  ┌────────┐ ┌────────┐ ┌────────┐       │        │
│  │  │Pipeline│ │Pipeline│ │Pipeline│       │        │
│  │  │  1     │ │  2     │ │  N     │       │        │
│  │  └────────┘ └────────┘ └────────┘       │        │
│  └──────────────────┬───────────────────────┘        │
│                     │                                 │
│  ┌──────────────────┴───────────────────────┐        │
│  │         Operator Runtime                  │        │
│  │  ┌────┐┌────┐┌────┐┌────┐┌────┐┌────┐  │        │
│  │  │Scan││Filt││Proj││Join││Agg ││Sort│  │        │
│  │  └────┘└────┘└────┘└────┘└────┘└────┘  │        │
│  └──────────────────┬───────────────────────┘        │
│                     │                                 │
│  ┌──────────────────┴───────────────────────┐        │
│  │         Memory Manager                    │        │
│  │  ┌────────┐ ┌────────┐ ┌────────┐       │        │
│  │  │Pool    │ │Spill   │ │Tracker │       │        │
│  │  │Manager │ │Manager │ │        │       │        │
│  │  └────────┘ └────────┘ └────────┘       │        │
│  └──────────────────┬───────────────────────┘        │
│                     │                                 │
│  ┌──────────────────┴───────────────────────┐        │
│  │         Shuffle Service                   │        │
│  │  ┌────────┐ ┌────────┐ ┌────────┐       │        │
│  │  │Shuffle │ │Shuffle │ │Shuffle │       │        │
│  │  │Client  │ │Server  │ │Cache   │       │        │
│  │  └────────┘ └────────┘ └────────┘       │        │
│  └──────────────────────────────────────────┘        │
└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
```

#### Pipeline 执行模型

AE 采用 Pipeline 执行模型，将查询计划分解为多个 Pipeline，每个 Pipeline 包含一组可以流水线执行的算子。

```
查询计划 → Pipeline 分解：

Logical Plan:
    Agg (Global)
      |
    Exchange (Hash Partition)
      |
    Agg (Local)
      |
    Filter
      |
    Scan

Pipeline 分解：
┌──────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│ Pipeline 1 (Map):                             │
│   Scan → Filter → LocalAgg → ShuffleWriter   │
│   (可流水线执行，无需物化中间结果)              │
├──────────────────────────────────────────────┤
│ Pipeline 2 (Reduce):                          │
│   ShuffleReader → GlobalAgg → ResultWriter   │
│   (需等待 Shuffle 数据就绪)                    │
└──────────────────────────────────────────────┘
```

```rust
pub struct Pipeline {
    id: PipelineId,
    operators: Vec<Box<dyn Operator>>,
    input_type: PipelineInputType,
    output_type: PipelineOutputType,
    parallelism: usize,
}

pub enum PipelineInputType {
    Scan(SourceSplit),
    Shuffle(ShuffleInput),
    Pipeline(PipelineId),
}

pub enum PipelineOutputType {
    Shuffle(ShuffleOutput),
    Sink(SinkSpec),
    Pipeline(PipelineId),
}

impl Pipeline {
    pub fn execute(&mut self, context: &mut ExecutionContext) -> Result<ExecutionResult, ExecutionError> {
        let mut input_iter = self.create_input(context)?;
        
        for batch in input_iter {
            let mut current_batch = batch?;
            
            for operator in &mut self.operators {
                current_batch = operator.process(current_batch, context)?;
                
                if current_batch.num_rows() == 0 {
                    break;
                }
            }
            
            self.output(current_batch, context)?;
        }
        
        for operator in &mut self.operators {
            operator.finish(context)?;
        }
        
        Ok(ExecutionResult::Completed)
    }
}
```

#### 算子接口

```rust
pub trait Operator: Send + Sync {
    fn name(&self) -> &str;
    fn schema(&self) -> &Schema;
    fn process(
        &mut self,
        batch: RecordBatch,
        context: &mut ExecutionContext,
    ) -> Result<RecordBatch, ExecutionError>;
    fn finish(&mut self, context: &mut ExecutionContext) -> Result<(), ExecutionError>;
    fn metrics(&self) -> OperatorMetrics;
    fn memory_usage(&self) -> MemoryUsage;
    fn can_spill(&self) -> bool;
    fn spill(&mut self, context: &mut ExecutionContext) -> Result<(), ExecutionError>;
}

pub struct FilterOperator {
    predicate: Arc<dyn PhysicalExpr>,
    schema: Schema,
    metrics: FilterMetrics,
}

impl Operator for FilterOperator {
    fn name(&self) -> &str { "Filter" }
    
    fn schema(&self) -> &Schema { &self.schema }
    
    fn process(
        &mut self,
        batch: RecordBatch,
        context: &mut ExecutionContext,
    ) -> Result<RecordBatch, ExecutionError> {
        let start = Instant::now();
        let mask = self.predicate.evaluate(&batch)?.as_boolean()?;
        let filtered = batch.filter(&mask)?;
        self.metrics.input_rows += batch.num_rows();
        self.metrics.output_rows += filtered.num_rows();
        self.metrics.cpu_time += start.elapsed();
        Ok(filtered)
    }
    
    fn finish(&mut self, _context: &mut ExecutionContext) -> Result<(), ExecutionError> {
        Ok(())
    }
    
    fn metrics(&self) -> OperatorMetrics {
        OperatorMetrics {
            name: self.name().to_string(),
            metrics: vec![
                Metric::Counter("input_rows", self.metrics.input_rows),
                Metric::Counter("output_rows", self.metrics.output_rows),
                Metric::Duration("cpu_time", self.metrics.cpu_time),
            ],
        }
    }
    
    fn memory_usage(&self) -> MemoryUsage { MemoryUsage::zero() }
    fn can_spill(&self) -> bool { false }
    fn spill(&mut self, _context: &mut ExecutionContext) -> Result<(), ExecutionError> { Ok(()) }
}
```

#### Hash Join 算子实现

```rust
pub struct HashJoinOperator {
    join_type: JoinType,
    left_keys: Vec<Arc<dyn PhysicalExpr>>,
    right_keys: Vec<Arc<dyn PhysicalExpr>>,
    condition: Option<Arc<dyn PhysicalExpr>>,
    schema: Schema,
    build_side: JoinBuildSide,
    state: HashJoinState,
    metrics: HashJoinMetrics,
    memory_manager: Arc<MemoryManager>,
}

enum HashJoinState {
    Building {
        hash_table: JoinHashTable,
        estimated_rows: usize,
    },
    Probing {
        hash_table: JoinHashTable,
        spilled_build: Option<SpilledPartition>,
    },
    Completed,
}

impl Operator for HashJoinOperator {
    fn name(&self) -> &str { "HashJoin" }
    
    fn process(
        &mut self,
        batch: RecordBatch,
        context: &mut ExecutionContext,
    ) -> Result<RecordBatch, ExecutionError> {
        match &mut self.state {
            HashJoinState::Building { hash_table, estimated_rows } => {
                hash_table.insert(batch, &self.left_keys)?;
                *estimated_rows += batch.num_rows();
                
                if self.memory_usage().bytes > self.memory_manager.spill_threshold() {
                    self.spill(context)?;
                }
                
                Ok(RecordBatch::empty(&self.schema))
            }
            HashJoinState::Probing { hash_table, .. } => {
                let result = hash_table.probe(batch, &self.right_keys, self.join_type)?;
                self.metrics.probe_rows += batch.num_rows();
                self.metrics.output_rows += result.num_rows();
                Ok(result)
            }
            HashJoinState::Completed => Ok(RecordBatch::empty(&self.schema)),
        }
    }
    
    fn finish(&mut self, context: &mut ExecutionContext) -> Result<(), ExecutionError> {
        if let HashJoinState::Building { hash_table, .. } = &self.state {
            let table = std::mem::take(hash_table);
            self.state = HashJoinState::Probing {
                hash_table: table,
                spilled_build: None,
            };
        }
        Ok(())
    }
    
    fn can_spill(&self) -> bool { true }
    
    fn spill(&mut self, context: &mut ExecutionContext) -> Result<(), ExecutionError> {
        if let HashJoinState::Building { hash_table, .. } = &mut self.state {
            let partitions = hash_table.spill_partitions(context.spill_manager())?;
            self.state = HashJoinState::Probing {
                hash_table: JoinHashTable::new(),
                spilled_build: Some(partitions),
            };
        }
        Ok(())
    }
    
    fn memory_usage(&self) -> MemoryUsage {
        match &self.state {
            HashJoinState::Building { hash_table, .. } => hash_table.memory_usage(),
            HashJoinState::Probing { hash_table, .. } => hash_table.memory_usage(),
            HashJoinState::Completed => MemoryUsage::zero(),
        }
    }
}
```

#### 内存管理器

```rust
pub struct MemoryManager {
    config: MemoryConfig,
    pools: RwLock<HashMap<MemoryPoolId, MemoryPool>>,
    global_tracker: AtomicUsize,
    spill_manager: SpillManager,
}

pub struct MemoryConfig {
    pub total_memory: usize,
    pub pool_initial_size: usize,
    pub pool_max_size: usize,
    pub spill_threshold: f64,
    pub oom_threshold: f64,
    pub reserved_memory: usize,
}

pub struct MemoryPool {
    id: MemoryPoolId,
    used: AtomicUsize,
    committed: AtomicUsize,
    limit: usize,
    listeners: Vec<Box<dyn MemoryListener>>,
}

impl MemoryManager {
    pub fn allocate(&self, pool_id: &MemoryPoolId, size: usize) -> Result<MemoryBlock, MemoryError> {
        let pools = self.pools.read();
        let pool = pools.get(pool_id).ok_or(MemoryError::PoolNotFound)?;
        
        let current = pool.used.load(Ordering::Relaxed);
        if current + size > pool.limit {
            self.trigger_spill(pool_id, size)?;
        }
        
        pool.used.fetch_add(size, Ordering::Relaxed);
        self.global_tracker.fetch_add(size, Ordering::Relaxed);
        
        Ok(MemoryBlock {
            ptr: self.allocate_raw(size)?,
            size,
            pool_id: pool_id.clone(),
        })
    }
    
    pub fn deallocate(&self, block: MemoryBlock) {
        let pools = self.pools.read();
        if let Some(pool) = pools.get(&block.pool_id) {
            pool.used.fetch_sub(block.size, Ordering::Relaxed);
        }
        self.global_tracker.fetch_sub(block.size, Ordering::Relaxed);
        self.deallocate_raw(block.ptr, block.size);
    }
    
    fn trigger_spill(&self, pool_id: &MemoryPoolId, required: usize) -> Result<(), MemoryError> {
        let pools = self.pools.read();
        if let Some(pool) = pools.get(pool_id) {
            for listener in &pool.listeners {
                let freed = listener.on_memory_pressure(required)?;
                if freed >= required {
                    return Ok(());
                }
            }
        }
        Err(MemoryError::OutOfMemory)
    }
}
```

#### Shuffle 服务

```
Shuffle 数据流：

Producer Worker                    Consumer Worker
┌──────────────┐                   ┌──────────────┐
│ Pipeline 1   │                   │ Pipeline 2   │
│              │                   │              │
│ ┌──────────┐ │    Arrow Flight   │ ┌──────────┐ │
│ │Shuffle   │ │═════════════════>│ │Shuffle   │ │
│ │Writer    │ │    RPC (gRPC)    │ │Reader    │ │
│ └──────────┘ │                   │ └──────────┘ │
│              │                   │              │
│ ┌──────────┐ │                   │ ┌──────────┐ │
│ │Local     │ │                   │ │Local     │ │
│ │Buffer    │ │                   │ │Buffer    │ │
│ └──────────┘ │                   │ └──────────┘ │
└──────────────┘                   └──────────────┘

Shuffle 流程：
1. ShuffleWriter 将数据按分区键 Hash 分区
2. 数据批量发送到目标 Worker（Arrow Flight RPC）
3. 目标 Worker 接收并缓存在本地 Buffer
4. ShuffleReader 按需读取本地 Buffer
5. 支持远程读取（当目标 Worker 不可用时）
```

```rust
pub struct ShuffleWriter {
    partition_count: usize,
    partition_hasher: PartitionHasher,
    buffers: Vec<ShuffleBuffer>,
    sender: ShuffleSender,
    metrics: ShuffleMetrics,
}

impl ShuffleWriter {
    pub fn write(&mut self, batch: RecordBatch) -> Result<(), ShuffleError> {
        let partitions = self.partition(&batch)?;
        
        for (partition_id, partition_batch) in partitions {
            if self.buffers[partition_id].should_flush() {
                self.flush(partition_id)?;
            }
            self.buffers[partition_id].write(partition_batch)?;
        }
        
        Ok(())
    }
    
    fn partition(&self, batch: &RecordBatch) -> Result<Vec<(usize, RecordBatch)>, ShuffleError> {
        let mut partition_masks: Vec<BooleanArray> = vec![BooleanArray::new_null(batch.num_rows()); self.partition_count];
        
        for i in 0..batch.num_rows() {
            let hash = self.partition_hasher.hash_row(batch, i);
            let partition = (hash % self.partition_count as u64) as usize;
            partition_masks[partition].set(i, true);
        }
        
        let mut result = Vec::new();
        for (pid, mask) in partition_masks.into_iter().enumerate() {
            let filtered = batch.filter(&mask)?;
            if filtered.num_rows() > 0 {
                result.push((pid, filtered));
            }
        }
        
        Ok(result)
    }
    
    fn flush(&mut self, partition_id: usize) -> Result<(), ShuffleError> {
        let data = self.buffers[partition_id].drain()?;
        self.sender.send(partition_id, data)?;
        Ok(())
    }
}
```

### 2.2.4 存储层（Storage Layer）

#### 概述

存储层提供统一的数据存储抽象，包括元数据存储、文件系统访问、缓存管理和状态后端。

#### 组件架构

```
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│                   存储层架构                           │
│                                                       │

│  │  │Catalog   │  │Catalog   │             │        │

│  └──────────────────────────────────────────┘        │
│                                                       │
│  ┌──────────────────────────────────────────┐        │

│  │  ┌──────────┐  ┌──────────┐             │        │
│  │  │Local FS  │  │HDFS/S3   │             │        │
│  │  │          │  │/GCS/OSS  │             │        │
│  │  └──────────┘  └──────────┘             │        │
│  └──────────────────────────────────────────┘        │
│                                                       │
│  ┌──────────────────────────────────────────┐        │

│  │  ┌──────────┐  ┌──────────┐             │        │
│  │  │Metadata  │  │Data      │             │        │
│  │  │Cache     │  │Cache     │             │        │
│  │  └──────────┘  └──────────┘             │        │
│  └──────────────────────────────────────────┘        │
│                                                       │
│  ┌──────────────────────────────────────────┐        │
│  │           State Backend                   │        │
│  │  ┌──────────┐  ┌──────────┐             │        │

└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
```

#### 文件系统抽象

```rust
pub trait FileSystem: Send + Sync {
    fn open_file(&self, path: &FilePath) -> Result<Box<dyn FileReader>, IOError>;
    fn create_file(&self, path: &FilePath) -> Result<Box<dyn FileWriter>, IOError>;
    fn delete_file(&self, path: &FilePath) -> Result<(), IOError>;
    fn rename(&self, src: &FilePath, dst: &FilePath) -> Result<(), IOError>;
    fn exists(&self, path: &FilePath) -> Result<bool, IOError>;
    fn list_dir(&self, path: &FilePath) -> Result<Vec<FileStatus>, IOError>;
    fn get_status(&self, path: &FilePath) -> Result<FileStatus, IOError>;
}

pub trait FileReader: Send {
    fn read_at(&self, offset: u64, len: usize) -> Result<Bytes, IOError>;
    fn read_all(&self) -> Result<Bytes, IOError>;
    fn size(&self) -> u64;
}

pub trait FileWriter: Send {
    fn write(&mut self, data: &[u8]) -> Result<(), IOError>;
    fn flush(&mut self) -> Result<(), IOError>;
    fn close(&mut self) -> Result<(), IOError>;
}

pub struct FileStatus {
    pub path: FilePath,
    pub size: u64,
    pub is_dir: bool,
    pub modification_time: u64,
    pub replication: u32,
}
```

#### 缓存管理器

```rust
pub struct CacheManager {
    metadata_cache: Arc<MetadataCache>,
    data_cache: Arc<DataCache>,
    config: CacheConfig,
}

pub struct CacheConfig {
    pub metadata_cache_size: usize,
    pub data_cache_size: usize,
    pub cache_ttl: Duration,
    pub eviction_policy: EvictionPolicy,
}

pub enum EvictionPolicy {
    LRU,
    LFU,
    ARC,
}

pub struct DataCache {
    store: RwLock<LruCache<CacheKey, CacheEntry>>,
    size_tracker: AtomicUsize,
    max_size: usize,
}

impl DataCache {
    pub fn get(&self, key: &CacheKey) -> Option<CacheEntry> {
        let mut store = self.store.write();
        store.get(key).cloned()
    }
    
    pub fn put(&self, key: CacheKey, entry: CacheEntry) -> Result<(), CacheError> {
        let mut store = self.store.write();
        
        while self.size_tracker.load(Ordering::Relaxed) + entry.size() > self.max_size {
            if let Some((_, evicted)) = store.pop_lru() {
                self.size_tracker.fetch_sub(evicted.size(), Ordering::Relaxed);
            } else {
                break;
            }
        }
        
        self.size_tracker.fetch_add(entry.size(), Ordering::Relaxed);
        store.put(key, entry);
        Ok(())
    }
    
    pub fn invalidate(&self, key: &CacheKey) {
        let mut store = self.store.write();
        if let Some(evicted) = store.pop(key) {
            self.size_tracker.fetch_sub(evicted.size(), Ordering::Relaxed);
        }
    }
}
```

### 2.2.5 基础设施层（Infrastructure Layer）

#### 概述

基础设施层提供底层能力支撑，包括网络通信、安全模块、可观测性栈和部署框架。

#### 网络栈

```
网络栈分层：

┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│                   Application Layer                   │
│  ┌──────────┐  ┌──────────┐                        │
│  │gRPC      │  │Arrow     │                        │
│  │Services  │  │Flight RPC│                        │
│  └──────────┘  └──────────┘                        │
├─────────────────────────────────────────────────────┤
│                   Transport Layer                     │
│  ┌──────────┐  ┌──────────┐                        │
│  │HTTP/2    │  │gRPC Frame│                        │
│  │          │  │          │                        │
│  └──────────┘  └──────────┘                        │
├─────────────────────────────────────────────────────┤
│                   Security Layer                      │
│  ┌──────────┐  ┌──────────┐                        │
│  │TLS 1.3   │  │mTLS      │                        │
│  └──────────┘  └──────────┘                        │
├─────────────────────────────────────────────────────┤
│                   Network Layer                       │
│  ┌──────────┐  ┌──────────┐                        │
│  │TCP       │  │Connection│                        │
│  │          │  │Pool      │                        │
│  └──────────┘  └──────────┘                        │
└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
```

#### 安全模块

```rust
pub struct SecurityModule {
    tls_config: TlsConfig,
    auth_provider: Arc<dyn AuthProvider>,
    access_controller: Arc<dyn AccessController>,
    audit_logger: Arc<dyn AuditLogger>,
}

pub struct TlsConfig {
    pub enabled: bool,
    pub cert_path: String,
    pub key_path: String,
    pub ca_path: String,
    pub mtls_enabled: bool,
    pub min_tls_version: TlsVersion,
}

pub enum TlsVersion {
    V1_2,
    V1_3,
}

impl SecurityModule {
    pub fn authenticate(&self, credentials: &Credentials) -> Result<Identity, SecurityError> {
        self.auth_provider.authenticate(credentials)
    }
    
    pub fn authorize(&self, identity: &Identity, action: &Action) -> Result<bool, SecurityError> {
        let allowed = self.access_controller.check(identity, action)?;
        self.audit_logger.log_access(identity, action, allowed);
        Ok(allowed)
    }
}
```

#### 可观测性栈

```rust
pub struct ObservabilityStack {
    metrics_collector: Arc<MetricsCollector>,
    trace_collector: Arc<TraceCollector>,
    log_collector: Arc<LogCollector>,
    exporters: Vec<Box<dyn TelemetryExporter>>,
}

impl ObservabilityStack {
    pub fn record_metric(&self, metric: Metric) {
        self.metrics_collector.record(metric);
        for exporter in &self.exporters {
            exporter.export_metric(&metric);
        }
    }
    
    pub fn start_span(&self, name: &str) -> Span {
        self.trace_collector.start_span(name)
    }
    
    pub fn log(&self, level: LogLevel, message: &str, fields: Vec<(String, String)>) {
        let entry = LogEntry {
            timestamp: Utc::now(),
            level,
            message: message.to_string(),
            fields,
            trace_id: self.trace_collector.current_trace_id(),
        };
        self.log_collector.record(entry);
        for exporter in &self.exporters {
            exporter.export_log(&entry);
        }
    }
}
```

## 2.3 服务拓扑与依赖关系图

### 2.3.1 服务拓扑

```
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│                        AE 服务拓扑                                    │
│                                                                       │
│  ┌──────────────────┐  ┌──────────────────┐  ┌──────────────────┐  │
│  │  Coordinator-1   │  │  Coordinator-2   │  │  Coordinator-3   │  │
│  │  (Leader)        │  │  (Standby)       │  │  (Standby)       │  │
│  └────────┬─────────┘  └────────┬─────────┘  └────────┬─────────┘  │
│           │                      │                      │            │
│           └──────────────────────┼──────────────────────┘            │
│                                  │                                    │
│                    ┌─────────────┴─────────────┐                     │
│                    │      Raft Consensus       │                     │
│                    └─────────────┬─────────────┘                     │
│                                  │                                    │
│  ┌───────┬───────┬───────┬──────┴──────┬───────┬───────┬───────┐   │
│  │       │       │       │             │       │       │       │   │
│  v       v       v       v             v       v       v       v   │
│ ┌─────┐ ┌─────┐ ┌─────┐ ┌─────┐ ┌─────┐ ┌─────┐ ┌─────┐ ┌─────┐│
│ │W-01 │ │W-02 │ │W-03 │ │W-04 │ │W-05 │ │W-06 │ │W-07 │ │W-NN ││
│ └─────┘ └─────┘ └─────┘ └─────┘ └─────┘ └─────┘ └─────┘ └─────┘│
│                                                                       │
│  ┌──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐   │
│  │                    External Services                          │   │
│  │  ┌──────────┐ ┌──────────┐ ┌──────────┐ ┌──────────┐       │   │
│  │  │Hive Meta │ │S3/HDFS   │ │Kafka     │ │Prometheus│       │   │
│  │  │Store     │ │          │ │          │ │          │       │   │
│  │  └──────────┘ └──────────┘ └──────────┘ └──────────┘       │   │
│  └──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘   │
└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
```

### 2.3.2 组件依赖关系图

```
组件依赖关系（箭头表示依赖方向）：

JDBC/ODBC/REST ──────> Query Router ──────> SQL Engine
                                              │
                                              v
                                        Query Planner ──────> Metadata Manager
                                              │                      │
                                              v                      v
                                        Adaptive Scheduler ───> Resource Manager
                                              │                      │
                                              v                      v
                                        Task Dispatcher ──────> Worker Agent
                                              │
                                              v
                                        Pipeline Executor
                                              │
                              ┌───────────────┼───────────────┐
                              v               v               v
                         Operator        Memory          Shuffle
                         Runtime         Manager         Service
                              │               │               │
                              v               v               v
                         State            Cache            File
                         Backend          Manager          System
```

### 2.3.3 数据流图

```
查询数据流：

Client
  │
  │ SQL
  v
Query Router ──> SQL Parser ──> Analyzer ──> Optimizer
                                                │
                                                v
                                          Query Planner
                                                │
                                    ┌───────────┼───────────┐
                                    v           v           v
                               Fragment 1  Fragment 2  Fragment N
                                    │           │           │
                                    v           v           v
                               Task-1-1    Task-2-1    Task-N-1
                               Task-1-2    Task-2-2    Task-N-2
                               Task-1-M    Task-2-M    Task-N-M
                                    │           │           │
                                    v           v           v
                               Worker-1    Worker-2    Worker-K
                                    │           │           │
                                    └───────────┼───────────┘
                                                │
                                                v
                                          Result Assembly
                                                │
                                                v
                                           Client
```

## 2.4 核心数据结构定义

### 2.4.1 查询生命周期数据结构

```rust
pub struct QueryId(String);

pub struct QuerySubmission {
    pub sql: String,
    pub catalog: Option<String>,
    pub schema: Option<String>,
    pub session_properties: HashMap<String, String>,
    pub query_type: QueryType,
    pub priority: Priority,
    pub timeout: Option<Duration>,
    pub user_identity: Identity,
}

pub enum QueryType {
    Batch,
    Stream,
    Interactive,
    Auto,
}

pub struct QueryExecution {
    pub query_id: QueryId,
    pub submission: QuerySubmission,
    pub state: QueryState,
    pub plan: Option<PhysicalPlan>,
    pub fragments: Vec<PlanFragment>,
    pub tasks: HashMap<TaskId, TaskExecution>,
    pub metrics: QueryMetrics,
    pub created_at: DateTime<Utc>,
    pub started_at: Option<DateTime<Utc>>,
    pub finished_at: Option<DateTime<Utc>>,
}

pub enum QueryState {
    Queued,
    Planning,
    Scheduled,
    Running,
    Finishing,
    Completed,
    Failed,
    Cancelled,
}

pub struct QueryMetrics {
    pub total_rows: u64,
    pub total_bytes: u64,
    pub cpu_time_ms: u64,
    pub peak_memory_bytes: u64,
    pub shuffle_bytes: u64,
    pub spill_bytes: u64,
}
```

### 2.4.2 计划相关数据结构

```rust
pub struct PlanFragment {
    pub fragment_id: FragmentId,
    pub plan_root: Arc<PhysicalPlanNode>,
    pub partitioning: Partitioning,
    pub input_fragments: Vec<FragmentId>,
    pub output: FragmentOutput,
    pub estimated_stats: PlanStatistics,
}

pub enum Partitioning {
    Single,
    RoundRobin(usize),
    Hash { columns: Vec<usize>, num_partitions: usize },
    Range { columns: Vec<usize>, bounds: Vec<RangeBound> },
    All,
}

pub enum FragmentOutput {
    Shuffle { partition_count: usize },
    Sink(SinkSpec),
    ResultCollector,
}

pub struct PlanStatistics {
    pub estimated_rows: u64,
    pub estimated_bytes: u64,
    pub estimated_cpu: f64,
    pub estimated_memory: u64,
    pub estimated_network: u64,
}
```

### 2.4.3 任务相关数据结构

```rust
pub struct TaskId {
    pub query_id: QueryId,
    pub fragment_id: FragmentId,
    pub partition_id: usize,
}

pub struct TaskExecution {
    pub task_id: TaskId,
    pub state: TaskState,
    pub worker_id: WorkerId,
    pub attempt: u32,
    pub metrics: TaskMetrics,
    pub created_at: DateTime<Utc>,
    pub started_at: Option<DateTime<Utc>>,
    pub finished_at: Option<DateTime<Utc>>,
}

pub enum TaskState {
    Pending,
    Running,
    Finished,
    Failed { error: String },
    Cancelled,
    Spilled,
}

pub struct TaskMetrics {
    pub input_rows: u64,
    pub output_rows: u64,
    pub input_bytes: u64,
    pub output_bytes: u64,
    pub cpu_time_ms: u64,
    pub peak_memory_bytes: u64,
    pub spill_bytes: u64,
    pub shuffle_read_bytes: u64,
    pub shuffle_write_bytes: u64,
}
```

### 2.4.4 资源相关数据结构

```rust
pub struct ResourceSpec {
    pub cpu_cores: f64,
    pub memory_bytes: u64,
    pub gpu_cards: u32,
}

pub struct ResourcePool {
    pub pool_id: PoolId,
    pub name: String,
    pub quota: ResourceSpec,
    pub used: ResourceSpec,
    pub reserved: ResourceSpec,
    pub priority: Priority,
    pub max_concurrency: usize,
    pub current_concurrency: usize,
}

pub struct WorkerDescriptor {
    pub worker_id: WorkerId,
    pub address: String,
    pub port: u16,
    pub total_resources: ResourceSpec,
    pub used_resources: ResourceSpec,
    pub state: WorkerState,
    pub labels: HashMap<String, String>,
    pub last_heartbeat: DateTime<Utc>,
}

pub enum WorkerState {
    Active,
    Draining,
    Decommissioning,
    Unhealthy { reason: String },
    Lost,
}
```

---

## 2.5 配置管理体系

### 2.5.1 配置层级

```
配置层级（优先级从高到低）：

1. Session Properties (查询级别)
   ├── SET SESSION key = value
   └── 优先级最高，仅影响当前会话

2. Query Hints (查询级别)
   ├── SELECT /*+ hint */ ...
   └── 嵌入在 SQL 中的提示

3. Catalog Properties (目录级别)
   ├── CREATE CATALOG ... WITH (key = value)
   └── 特定目录的配置

4. Resource Pool Properties (资源池级别)
   ├── CREATE RESOURCE POOL ... WITH (key = value)
   └── 特定资源池的配置

5. Cluster Properties (集群级别)
   ├── ae-config.yaml
   └── 全局默认配置

6. System Defaults (系统默认)
   ├── 硬编码默认值
   └── 优先级最低
```

### 2.5.2 配置文件格式

```yaml
# ae-config.yaml - AE 集群配置文件

cluster:
  name: ae-production
  environment: production

coordinator:
  host: 0.0.0.0
  port: 8080
  grpc_port: 9090
  ha:
    enabled: true
    raft_peers:
      - coordinator-1:9090
      - coordinator-2:9090
      - coordinator-3:9090
    election_timeout: 5s
    heartbeat_interval: 1s

worker:
  host: 0.0.0.0
  data_port: 9091
  control_port: 9092
  heartbeat_interval: 5s
  max_heartbeat_miss: 3

scheduler:
  type: adaptive
  queue_types:
    - interactive
    - batch
    - stream
  interactive_queue:
    max_concurrency: 50
    timeout: 30s
    priority: HIGH
  batch_queue:
    max_concurrency: 20
    timeout: 3600s
    priority: MEDIUM
  stream_queue:
    max_concurrency: 100
    priority: HIGH
  adaptive:
    enabled: true
    feedback_interval: 10s
    skew_detection_threshold: 3.0
    auto_parallelism: true

memory:
  total_memory: 64GB
  pool_initial_fraction: 0.1
  pool_max_fraction: 0.8
  spill_threshold: 0.85
  oom_threshold: 0.95
  reserved_memory: 2GB

optimizer:
  max_iterations: 100
  cost_model: adaptive
  enable_join_reorder: true
  enable_predicate_pushdown: true
  enable_projection_pruning: true
  enable_adaptive_join: true

state:
  backend: ae-rocks
  checkpoint_interval: 30s
  checkpoint_timeout: 10min
  max_concurrent_checkpoints: 1
  incremental_checkpoint: true
  savepoint_dir: s3://ae-savepoints/

catalog:
  default: hive
  cache_ttl: 300s
  cache_max_size: 10000

security:
  authentication:
    enabled: true
    type: kerberos
  authorization:
    enabled: true
    type: rbac
  tls:
    enabled: true
    cert_path: /etc/ae/tls/server.crt
    key_path: /etc/ae/tls/server.key
    ca_path: /etc/ae/tls/ca.crt

observability:
  metrics:
    enabled: true
    export_interval: 15s
    prometheus_port: 9095
  tracing:
    enabled: true
    sample_rate: 0.1
    exporter: jaeger
    jaeger_endpoint: http://jaeger:14268/api/traces
  logging:
    level: INFO
    format: json
    output: /var/log/ae/ae.log
```

### 2.5.3 动态配置接口

```sql
-- 查询配置
SHOW SESSION;
SHOW SESSION LIKE 'scheduler%';

-- 设置会话配置
SET SESSION scheduler.adaptive.enabled = true;
SET SESSION optimizer.join_reorder = true;
SET SESSION memory.spill_threshold = 0.9;

-- 查询集群配置
SHOW CLUSTER CONFIG;
SHOW CLUSTER CONFIG LIKE 'state%';

-- 动态修改集群配置（需要管理员权限）
ALTER CLUSTER SET state.checkpoint_interval = '60s';
ALTER CLUSTER SET scheduler.adaptive.skew_detection_threshold = 5.0;
```

## 2.6 日志与可观测性架构

### 2.6.1 可观测性架构总览

```
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│                     AE 可观测性架构                                │
│                                                                   │
│  ┌──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐   │
│  │                    数据采集层                              │   │
│  │                                                            │   │

│  │  │Collector │  │Collector │  │Collector │  │Collector ││   │
│  │  └──────────┘  └──────────┘  └──────────┘  └──────────┘│   │

│                              │                                    │
│  ┌──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐   │
│  │                    数据处理层                              │   │
│  │                                                            │   │
│  │  ┌──────────┐  ┌──────────┐  ┌──────────┐  ┌──────────┐│   │
│  │  │Aggregator│  │Sampler   │  │Formatter │  │Enricher  ││   │
│  │  └──────────┘  └──────────┘  └──────────┘  └──────────┘│   │
│  └──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘   │
│                              │                                    │
│  ┌──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐   │
│  │                    数据存储层                              │   │
│  │                                                            │   │
│  │  ┌──────────┐  ┌──────────┐  ┌──────────┐  ┌──────────┐│   │
│  │  │Prometheus│  │Jaeger/   │  │Loki/ELK  │  │AE Internal││  │
│  │  │          │  │Tempo     │  │          │  │Store      ││   │
│  │  └──────────┘  └──────────┘  └──────────┘  └──────────┘│   │
```
